## TOPIC 00001: PowerList

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-powelist-mnu.html`

- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure PowerList measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties. icon

### PowerList

Use the VIs on this palette to configure PowerList measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-powelist-mnu.png']

- [RFmxSpecAn PowerList Configure RBW Filter (Array) VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-powerlist-configure-rbw-filter-array-vi.html) Configures array of the resolution bandwidth (RBW) filter to measure the power of the signal as seen through this filter, each corresponding to a segment.

Parent topic:

Configuration

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spectrum-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00002: Spectrum

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spectrum-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spectrum-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure Spectrum measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties. icon

### Spectrum

Use the VIs on this palette to configure Spectrum measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spectrum-mnu.png']

- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Span VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-span-vi.html) Configures the frequency range, in Hz, around the center frequency, to acquire for the spectrum measurement.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Frequency Start Stop VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-frequency-start-stop-vi.html) Configures the start frequency and stop frequency for the spectrum measurement.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Power Units VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-power-units-vi.html) Configures the units for the absolute power.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Noise Compensation Enabled VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-noise-compensation-enabled-vi.html) Configures compensation of the spectrum for the inherent noise floor of the signal analyzer.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure RBW Filter VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-rbw-filter-vi.html) Configures the resolution bandwidth (RBW) filter.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Measurement Method VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-measurement-method-vi.html) Configures the method for performing the Spectrum measurement.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Sweep Time VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-sweep-time-vi.html) Configures the sweep time.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Averaging VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-averaging-vi.html) Configures averaging for the spectrum measurement.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure FFT VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-fft-vi.html) Configures window and FFT to obtain a spectrum for the spectrum measurement.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure Detector VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-detector-vi.html) Configures the detector settings, including detector type and the number of points to be detected.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure VBW Filter VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-configure-vbw-filter-vi.html) Configures the VBW settings including VBW Auto, VBW(Hz) and VBW to RBW ratio.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Validate Noise Calibration Data VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spectrum-validate-noise-calibration-data-vi.html) Indicates whether calibration data is valid for the configuration specified by the signal name in the Selector string parameter.

Parent topic:

Configuration

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spur-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00003: Spur

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spur-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spur-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure spurious emission (Spur) measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties. icon

### Spur

Use the VIs on this palette to configure spurious emission (Spur) measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spur-mnu.png']

- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Number of Ranges VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-number-of-ranges-vi.html) Configures the number of ranges.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range Frequency VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-frequency-vi.html) Configures the frequency start and stop values of the range.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range RBW Filter VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-rbw-filter-vi.html) Configures the resolution bandwidth (RBW) filter.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range Sweep Time VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-sweep-time-vi.html) Configures the sweep time.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range Absolute Limit VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-absolute-limit-vi.html) Configures the absolute power limits corresponding to the beginning and end of the frequency range.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range Relative Attenuation VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-relative-attenuation-vi.html) Specifies the attenuation, in dB, relative to the external attenuation.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range Number of Spurs to Report VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-number-of-spurs-to-report-vi.html) Specifies the number of Spurs that the measurement should report in the frequency range.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Trace Range Index VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-trace-range-index-vi.html) Specifies the index of the range used to store and retrieve the spurious emission (Spur) trace.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range Peak Criteria VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-peak-criteria-vi.html) Configures the peak threshold and peak excursion criteria which a peak should meet to be classified as a spurious emission (Spur).
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Averaging VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-averaging-vi.html) Configures averaging for the spurious emission (Spur) measurement.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure FFT Window Type VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-fft-window-type-vi.html) Configures the FFT window to obtain a spectrum for the spurious emission (Spur) measurement.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range Detector VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-detector-vi.html) Configures the detector settings including detector type and the number of points to be detected.
- [RFmxSpecAn Spur Configure Range VBW Filter VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-spur-configure-range-vbw-filter-vi.html) Configures the video bandwidth (VBW) settings including VBW Auto, VBW, and VBW to RBW ratio for the specified range.
- [RFmxSpecAn Build Range String2 VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-build-range-string2-vi.html) Creates selector string for use with spurious emissions (Spur) configuration or fetch properties and VIs.
- [Spur Array VIs](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/rfmx-specan-mx-configuration-spur-array-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure spurious emission (Spur) measurements. You can use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.

Parent topic:

Configuration

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/dir-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00004: SpecAn

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/dir-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/dir-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to perform spectrum analysis measurements. You can use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties. © 2014–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved. icon

### SpecAn

Use the VIs on this palette to perform spectrum analysis measurements. You can use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.

© 2014–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='dir-mnu.png']

- [Configuration](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/configuration/dir-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure RFmxSpecAn measurements. You can use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.
- [RFmxSpecAn Read VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-read-vi.html) Configures hardware for acquisition, performs measurement on acquired data, and returns measurement results.
- [RFmxSpecAn Select Measurement VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-select-measurement-vi.html) Specifies the measurements that you want to enable. To select a single measurement, use the Single Measurement instance. To select multiple measurements, use the Multiple Measurements instance.
- [RFmxSpecAn Initiate VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-initiate-vi.html) Initiates all enabled measurements. Call this VI after configuring the signal and measurement. This VI asynchronously launches measurements in the background and immediately returns to the caller program. You can fetch measurement results using the Fetch VIs or result properties in the property node. To get the status of measurements, use the RFmxSpecAn Wait for Measurement Complete VI or RFmxSpecAn Check Measurement Status VI.
- [Fetch](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-fetch-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to fetch measurement results and traces.
- [Utility](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/utility/dir-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure RFmx SpecAn utilities.
- [Marker](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-markers-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure marker measurements.
- [Advanced](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-advanced-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to use advanced features.
- [RFmxSpecAn VI Tree VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-vi-tree-vi.html) Displays all the VIs available in RFmxSpecAn for measurement configuration and fetching results. The VIs are organized in the order they must be used in the program you create.
- [RFmxSpecAn Property Node VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-property-node-vi.html) Gets (reads), sets (writes), or resets (sets to default value) RFmxSpecAn properties.
- [Build String](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/utility/rfmx-specan-mx-utility-build-string-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to create strings for configurations and results that require a selector string.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-apply-dpd-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00005: Apply DPD

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-apply-dpd-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-apply-dpd-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to apply DPD measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties. icon

### Apply DPD

Use the VIs on this palette to apply DPD measurements. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-specan-mx-apply-dpd-mnu.png']

- [RFmxSpecAn DPD Configure Apply DPD Configuration Input VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-dpd-configure-apply-dpd-configuration-input-vi.html) Configures the source of measurement settings for applying DPD.
- [RFmxSpecAn DPD Configure Apply DPD Lookup Table Correction Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-dpd-configure-apply-dpd-lookup-table-correction-type-vi.html) Configures the predistortion type when you set the DPD Model property to Lookup Table .
- [RFmxSpecAn DPD Configure Apply DPD Memory Models Correction Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-dpd-configure-apply-dpd-memory-models-correction-type-vi.html) Configures the predistortion type when you set the DPD Model property to Memory Polynomial or Generalized Memory Polynomial .
- [RFmxSpecAn DPD Apply Digital Predistortion VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-dpd-apply-digital-predistortion-vi.html) Scales the input waveform to DUT average input power and then predistorts using the DPD polynomial or the lookup table. To scale the waveform correctly, specify if the idle duration is present in the waveform.
- [RFmxSpecAn DPD Fetch Apply DPD Pre-CFR PAPR VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-dpd-fetch-apply-dpd-pre-cfr-papr-vi.html) Fetches the PAPR of the pre-distorted waveform before CFR is applied to it.
- [User DPD](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-user-dpd-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the DPD Lookup Table or DPD Polynomial for applying DPD. You can also use the RFmxSpecAn Property Node to configure additional properties.

Parent topic:

Fetch

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-markers-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00006: Marker

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-markers-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/specan/rfmx-specan-mx-markers-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure marker measurements. icon

### Marker

Use the VIs on this palette to configure marker measurements.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-specan-mx-markers-mnu.png']

- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Number of Markers VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-number-of-markers-vi.html) Configures the number of markers.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-type-vi.html) Configures the marker type.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Trace VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-trace-vi.html) Configures the measurement trace to be used by the marker.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Reference Marker VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-reference-marker-vi.html) Configures the reference marker to a delta marker.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Y Location VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-y-location-vi.html) Configures the Y location of the marker. You must configure the reference marker Y location or perform peak search on the reference marker before configuring the X location for the Delta marker.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure X Location VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-x-location-vi.html) Configures the X location of the marker. You must configure the reference marker X location or perform peak search on the reference marker before configuring the X location for the Delta marker.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Threshold VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-threshold-vi.html) Configures the threshold to use for peak search.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Peak Excursion VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-peak-excursion-vi.html) Configures the peak excursion.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Function Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-function-type-vi.html) Configures the marker function type.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Configure Band Span VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-configure-band-span-vi.html) Configures the band span of the selected marker.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Peak Search VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-peak-search-vi.html) Moves the marker to the highest peak that satisfies peak threshold and peak excursion criteria.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Next Peak VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-next-peak-vi.html) Moves the marker to the next highest or next left or next right peak above the threshold on the configured trace.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Fetch XY VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-fetch-xy-vi.html) Returns the X and Y locations of the marker.
- [RFmxSpecAn Marker Fetch Function Value VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-marker-fetch-function-value-vi.html) Returns the function value of the selected marker function type.
- [RFmxSpecAn Build Marker String2 VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-build-marker-string2-vi.html) Creates selector string for use with marker configuration or fetch properties and VIs.

Parent topic:

SpecAn

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100002.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00007: Reference Level

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100002.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100002.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the reference level which represents the maximum expected power of the RF input signal. This value is configured in dBm for RF devices and as Vpk-pk for baseband devices. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to t

### Reference Level

Specifies the reference level which represents the maximum expected power of the RF input signal. This value is configured in dBm for RF devices and as Vpk-pk for baseband devices.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default of this property is hardware dependent.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Reference Level |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn Configure Reference Level |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100003.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00008: External Attenuation (dB)

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100003.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100003.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the attenuation of a switch (or cable) connected to the RF IN connector of the signal analyzer. This value is expressed in dB. For more information about attenuation, refer to the Attenuation and Signal Levels topic for your device in the NI RF Vector Signal Analyzers Help. You do not need

### External Attenuation (dB)

Specifies the attenuation of a switch (or cable) connected to the RF IN connector of the signal analyzer. This value is expressed in dB. For more information about attenuation, refer to the Attenuation and Signal Levels topic for your device in the *NI RF Vector Signal Analyzers Help*.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is 0.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | External Attenuation (dB) |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn Configure External Attenuation |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100006.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00009: Trigger:Digital Edge:Edge

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100006.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100006.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the active edge for the trigger. This property is used only when you set the Trigger Type property to Digital Edge. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the str

### Trigger:Digital Edge:Edge

Specifies the active edge for the trigger. This property is used only when you set the [Trigger Type](/csh?topicname=attr100004.html) property to **Digital Edge**.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Rising Edge**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Digital Edge |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn Configure Trigger |
| Resettable | Yes |

| Rising Edge | 0 | The trigger asserts on the rising edge of the signal. |
| --- | --- | --- |

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`

### Trigger:IQ Power Edge:Slope

Specifies whether the device asserts the trigger when the signal power is rising or when it is falling. The device asserts the trigger when the signal power exceeds the specified level with the slope you specify. This property is used only when you set the [Trigger Type](/csh?topicname=attr100004.html) property to **IQ Power Edge**.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Rising Slope**.

| Resettable | Yes |

| Rising Slope | 0 | The trigger asserts when the signal power is rising. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Falling Slope | 1 | The trigger asserts when the signal power is falling. |

## TOPIC 00015: Reference Level Headroom

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100ffc.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr100ffc.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the margin RFmx adds to the Reference Level property. The margin avoids clipping and overflow warnings if the input signal exceeds the configured reference level. RFmx configures the input gain to avoid clipping and associated overflow warnings provided the instantaneous power of the input

### Reference Level Headroom

Specifies the margin RFmx adds to the [Reference Level](/csh?topicname=attr100002.html) property. The margin avoids clipping and overflow warnings if the input signal exceeds the configured reference level.

RFmx configures the input gain to avoid clipping and associated overflow warnings provided the instantaneous power of the input signal remains within the Reference Level plus the Reference Level Headroom. If you know the input power of the signal precisely or previously included the margin in the Reference Level, you could improve the signal-to-noise ratio by reducing the Reference Level Headroom.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

**Supported devices:**PXIe-5668, PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860.

**Default values**

| PXIe-5668 | 6 dB |
| --- | --- |
| PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5841/5842/5860 | 1 dB |
| PXIe-5840 | 0 dB |

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Reference Level Headroom |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

## TOPIC 00021: CHP:FFT:Window

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10300a.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10300a.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the FFT window type to use to reduce spectral leakage. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax for named signals. The default value is Flat Top.

### CHP:FFT:Window

Specifies the FFT window type to use to reduce spectral leakage.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Flat Top**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CHP FFT Window |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn CHP Configure FFT |
| Resettable | Yes |

| None | 0 | Analyzes transients for which duration is shorter than the window length. You can also use this window type to separate two tones with frequencies close to each other but with almost equal amplitudes. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Flat Top | 1 | Measures single-tone amplitudes accurately. |
| Hanning | 2 | Analyzes transients for which duration is longer than the window length. You can also use this window type to provide better frequency resolution for noise measurements. |
| Hamming | 3 | Analyzes closely-spaced sine waves. |
| Gaussian | 4 | Provides a good balance of spectral leakage, frequency resolution, and amplitude attenuation. Hence, this windowing is useful for time-frequency analysis. |
| Blackman | 5 | Analyzes single tone because it has a low maximum side lobe level and a high side lobe roll-off rate. |
| Blackman-Harris | 6 | Useful as a good general purpose window, having side lobe rejection greater than 90 dB and having a moderately wide main lobe. |
| Kaiser-Bessel | 7 | Separates two tones with frequencies close to each other but with widely-differing amplitudes. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

## TOPIC 00022: CHP:FFT:Padding

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10300b.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10300b.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the factor by which the time-domain waveform is zero-padded before fast Fourier transform (FFT). The FFT size is given by the following formula: waveform size * padding This property is used only when the acquisition span is less than the device instantaneous bandwidth of the device. You d

### CHP:FFT:Padding

Specifies the factor by which the time-domain waveform is zero-padded before fast Fourier transform (FFT). The FFT size is given by the following formula:

waveform size * padding

This property is used only when the acquisition span is less than the device instantaneous bandwidth of the device.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is -1.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CHP FFT Padding |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn CHP Configure FFT |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

## TOPIC 00024: CHP:Detector:Type

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr103013.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr103013.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`

- source_description: Specifies the type of detector to be used. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax for named signals. The default value is None. Refer to Spectral Measurem

### CHP:Detector:Type

Specifies the type of detector to be used.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **None**.

Refer to [Spectral Measurements](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_spectral_measurements_concepts) topic for more information on detector types.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CHP Detector Type |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| None | 0 | The detector is disabled. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Sample | 1 | The middle sample in the bucket is detected. |
| Normal | 2 | The maximum value of the samples within the bucket is detected if the signal only rises or if the signal only falls. If the signal, within a bucket, both rises and falls, then the maximum and minimum values of the samples are detected in alternate buckets. |
| Peak | 3 | The maximum value of the samples in the bucket is detected. |
| Negative Peak | 4 | The minimum value of the samples in the bucket is detected. |
| Average RMS | 5 | The average RMS of all the samples in the bucket is detected. |
| Average Voltage | 6 | The average voltage of all the samples in the bucket is detected. |
| Average Log | 7 | The average log of all the samples in the bucket is detected. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

### CHP:Measurement Mode

Specifies whether the measurement calibrates the noise floor of analyzer or performs the CHP measurement. Refer to the measurement guidelines section in the [Noise Compensation Algorithm](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_noise_compensation_algorithm) topic for more information.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Measure**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CHP Meas Mode |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| Measure | 0 | CHP measurement is performed on the acquired signal. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Calibrate Noise Floor | 1 | Manual noise calibration of the signal analyzer is performed for the CHP measurement. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

## TOPIC 00031: FCnt:Number of Analysis Threads

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr104003.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr104003.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for FCnt measurement. The number of threads can range from 1 to the number of physical cores. The number of threads you set may not be used in calculations. The actual number of threads used depends on the problem size, system resources, d

### FCnt:Number of Analysis Threads

Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for FCnt measurement.

The number of threads can range from 1 to the number of physical cores. The number of threads you set may not be used in calculations. The actual number of threads used depends on the problem size, system resources, data availability, and other considerations.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is 1.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | FCnt Num Analysis Threads |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn FCnt Configure RBW Filter |
| Resettable | Yes |

| None | 5 | The measurement does not use any RBW filtering. |

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is 0.001.

**Supported devices**: PXIe-5665/5668

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Harm Fundamental Meas Interval (s) |

| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn Harm Configure Fundamental Measurement Interval |
| Resettable | Yes |

### Harm:Harmonic:Enabled

Specifies whether to enable a particular harmonic for measurement. Only the enabled harmonics are used to measure the total harmonic distortion (THD). This property is not used if you set the [Harm Harmonics Auto Setup Enabled](/csh?topicname=attr105008.html) to **True**.

Use "harmonic<*n*>" as the [selector string](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) to configure or read this property.

The default value is **True**.

| Resettable | Yes |

| False | 0 | Disables the harmonic for measurement. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| True | 1 | Enables the harmonic for measurement. |

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10500f.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10500f.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the averaging type for the Harmonics measurement. The averaged power trace is used for the measurement. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax f

### Harm:Averaging:Type

Specifies the averaging type for the Harmonics measurement. The averaged power trace is used for the measurement.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **RMS**.

**Supported devices**: PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5663/5663E/5665/5668

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Harm Averaging Type |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn Harm Configure Averaging |
| Resettable | Yes |

| RMS | 0 | The power trace is linearly averaged. RMS averaging reduces signal fluctuations but not the noise floor. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Log | 1 | The power trace is averaged in a logarithmic scale. |
| Scalar | 2 | The square root of the power trace is averaged. |
| Max | 3 | The maximum instantaneous power in the power trace is retained from one acquisition to the next. |
| Min | 4 | The minimum instantaneous power in the power trace is retained from one acquisition to the next. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

- source_description: Returns the total harmonics distortion (THD), measured as a percentage of the power in the fundamental signal. THD (%) = SQRT (Total power of all enabled harmonics - Power in fundamental) * 100 / Power in fundamental You do not need to use a selector string to read this result for default signal and

### Harm:Results:Total Harmonic Distortion (%)

Returns the total harmonics distortion (THD), measured as a percentage of the power in the fundamental signal.

THD (%) = SQRT (Total power of all enabled harmonics - Power in fundamental) * 100 / Power in fundamental

You do not need to use a selector string to read this result for default signal and result instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals and results.

| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |

| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn Harm Fetch Fundamental Measurement |
| Resettable | No |

- source_description: Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for the OBW measurement. The number of threads can range from 1 to the number of physical cores. The number of threads you set may not be used in calculations. The actual number of threads used depends on the problem size, system resources

### OBW:Number of Analysis Threads

Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for the OBW measurement.

The number of threads can range from 1 to the number of physical cores. The number of threads you set may not be used in calculations. The actual number of threads used depends on the problem size, system resources, data availability, and other considerations.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is 1.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | OBW Num Analysis Threads |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

### OBW:Results:Average Power (dBm or dBm/Hz)

| --- | --- | --- |
| Trigger | 1 | The measurement is performed across segments obtained in multiple records, where each record is obtained when a trigger is received. The number of segments is equal to the number of triggers (records). |

## TOPIC 00059: PAVT:Results:Mean Relative Phase (deg)

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10700a.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10700a.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Returns the mean phase of the segment, relative to the phase of the reference segment. This value is expressed in degrees. Mean Relative Phase = Qi - Qr Qi is the absolute phase of the segment i, expressed in degrees Qr is the absolute phase of the reference segment r, expressed in degrees where, r

### PAVT:Results:Mean Relative Phase (deg)

Returns the mean phase of the segment, relative to the phase of the reference segment. This value is expressed in degrees.

Mean Relative Phase = Qi - Qr

Qi is the absolute phase of the segment i, expressed in degrees

Qr is the absolute phase of the reference segment r, expressed in degrees

where,

r = 1, if Segment0 is configured as Frequency Error Measurement segment

r = 0, otherwise

Use "segment<*n*>" as the [selector string](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) to read this result.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | PAVT Results Mean Rel Phase (deg) |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read Only |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | No |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

Use "carrier<*n*>" as the [selector string](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) to configure or read this property.

The default value is 0.1.

### SEM:Averaging:Type

Specifies the averaging type for averaging multiple spectrum acquisitions. The averaged spectrum is used for SEM measurement.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **RMS**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | SEM Averaging Type |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn SEM Configure Averaging |
| Resettable | Yes |

| RMS | 0 | The power spectrum is linearly averaged. RMS averaging reduces signal fluctuations but not the noise floor. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Log | 1 | The power spectrum is averaged in a logarithmic scale. |
| Scalar | 2 | The square root of the power spectrum is averaged. |
| Max | 3 | The peak power in the spectrum at each frequency bin is retained from one acquisition to the next. |
| Min | 4 | The least power in the spectrum at each frequency bin is retained from one acquisition to the next. |

RFmxSpecAn Properties

## TOPIC 00077: SEM:FFT:Window

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr108022.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr108022.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the FFT window type to use to reduce spectral leakage. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax for named signals. The default value is Flat Top.

### SEM:FFT:Window

Specifies the FFT window type to use to reduce spectral leakage.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Flat Top**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | SEM FFT Window |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn SEM Configure FFT |
| Resettable | Yes |

| None | 0 | Analyzes transients for which duration is shorter than the window length. You can also use this window type to separate two tones with frequencies close to each other but with almost equal amplitudes. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Flat Top | 1 | Measures single-tone amplitudes accurately. |
| Hanning | 2 | Analyzes transients for which duration is longer than the window length. You can also use this window type to provide better frequency resolution for noise measurements. |
| Hamming | 3 | Analyzes closely-spaced sine waves. |
| Gaussian | 4 | Provides a good balance of spectral leakage, frequency resolution, and amplitude attenuation. Hence, this windowing is useful for time-frequency analysis. |
| Blackman | 5 | Analyzes single tone because it has a low maximum side lobe level and a high side lobe roll-off rate. |
| Blackman-Harris | 6 | Useful as a good general purpose window, having side lobe rejection greater than 90 dB and having a moderately wide main lobe. |
| Kaiser-Bessel | 7 | Separates two tones with frequencies close to each other but with widely-differing amplitudes. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

### SEM:FFT:Padding

Specifies the factor by which the time-domain waveform is zero-padded before FFT. The FFT size is given by the following formula:

waveform size * padding

This property is used only when the acquisition span is less than the device instantaneous bandwidth of the device.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is -1.

### SEM:Results:Composite Measurement Status

Indicates the overall measurement status based on the measurement limits and the fail criteria that you set in the [SEM Offset Limit Fail Mask](/csh?topicname=attr10800d.html) property for each offset segment.

You do not need to use a selector string to read this result for default signal and result instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals and results.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | SEM Results Meas Status |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read Only |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn SEM Fetch Composite Measurement Status |
| Resettable | No |

| Fail | 0 | Indicates that the measurement has failed. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Pass | 1 | Indicates that the measurement has passed. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

### SEM:Results:Lower Offset:Peak Relative Power (dB)

Returns the peak power measured in the lower (negative) offset segment relative to the integrated or peak power of the reference carrier.

When you set the [SEM Ref Type](attr108024.html) property to **Integration**, the reference carrier power is the total power in the reference carrier. When you set the SEM Ref Type property to **Peak**, the reference carrier power is the peak power in the reference carrier.

Use "offset<*n*>" as the [selector string](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) to read this result.

#### Remarks

| Resettable | No |

Use "carrier<n>" as

### SEM:Carrier:Channel Bandwidth (Hz)

specifies the channel bandwidth of the carrier. This parameter is used to calculate the values of the [SEM Offset Start Freq](/csh?topicname=attr108014.html) and [SEM Offset Stop Freq](/csh?topicname=attr108015.html) properties when you set the [SEM Offset Freq Definition](/csh?topicname=attr10804c.html) property to **Carrier Edge to Meas BW Center** or **Carrier Edge to Meas BW Edge**.

Use "carrier<*n*>" as the [selector string](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) to configure or read this property.

The default value is 2 MHz.

## TOPIC 00099: SEM:Amplitude Correction Type

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10804f.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10804f.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether the amplitude of the frequency bins, used in the measurement, is corrected for external attenuation at the RF center frequency, or at the individual frequency bins. Use the RFmxInstr Configure External Attenuation Table VI to configure the external attenuation table. You do not nee

### SEM:Amplitude Correction Type

Specifies whether the amplitude of the frequency bins, used in the measurement, is corrected for external attenuation at the RF center frequency, or at the individual frequency bins. Use the [RFmxInstr Configure External Attenuation Table](/csh?context=rfmxinstr_rfmxinstrvi_rfmxinstr_configure_external_attenuation_table) VI to configure the external attenuation table.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **RF Center Frequency**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | SEM Amplitude Correction Type |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| RF Center Frequency | 0 | All the frequency bins in the spectrum are compensated with a single external attenuation value that corresponds to the RF center frequency. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Spectrum Frequency Bin | 1 | An individual frequency bin in the spectrum is compensated with the external attenuation value corresponding to that frequency. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

## TOPIC 00101: Spectrum:FFT:Window

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr109009.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr109009.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the FFT window type to use to reduce spectral leakage. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax for named signals. The default value is Flat Top.

### Spectrum:FFT:Window

Specifies the FFT window type to use to reduce spectral leakage.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Flat Top**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Spectrum FFT Window |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | RFmxSpecAn Spectrum Configure FFT |
| Resettable | Yes |

| None | 0 | Analyzes transients for which duration is shorter than the window length. You can also use this window type to separate two tones with frequencies close to each other but with almost equal amplitudes. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Flat Top | 1 | Measures single-tone amplitudes accurately. |
| Hanning | 2 | Analyzes transients for which duration is longer than the window length. You can also use this window type to provide better frequency resolution for noise measurements. |
| Hamming | 3 | Analyzes closely-spaced sine waves. |
| Gaussian | 4 | Provides a good balance of spectral leakage, frequency resolution, and amplitude attenuation. Hence, this windowing is useful for time-frequency analysis. |
| Blackman | 5 | Analyzes single tone because it has a low maximum side lobe level and a high side lobe roll-off rate. |
| Blackman-Harris | 6 | Useful as a good general purpose window, having side lobe rejection greater than 90 dB and having a moderately wide main lobe. |
| Kaiser-Bessel | 7 | Separates two tones with frequencies close to each other but with widely-differing amplitudes. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10900b.html language=enus -->

### Spectrum:Results:Peak Amplitude (dBm)

Returns the peak amplitude, of the averaged spectrum.

When you set the [Spectrum Span](attr109003.html) property to 0, the measurement returns the peak amplitude in the time domain power trace.

The amplitude is reported in units specified by the value of the [Spectrum Power Units](attr109015.html) property.

You do not need to use a selector string to read this result for default signal and result instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals and results.

| Resettable | No |

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax for named signals. The

### AMPM:Synchronization Method

Specifies the method used for synchronization of acquired waveform with reference waveform.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Direct**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AMPM Sync Method |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| Direct | 1 | Synchronizes the acquired and reference waveforms assuming that sample rate is sufficient to prevent aliasing in intermediate operations. This method is recommended when the measurement sampling rate is high. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Alias Protected | 2 | Synchronizes the acquired and reference waveforms while ascertaining that intermediate operations are not impacted by aliasing. This method is recommended for non-contiguous carriers separated by a large gap, and/or when the measurement sampling rate is low. Refer to AMPM concept help for more information. |

Parent topic:

| Short Name | AMPM Threshold Definition |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| Input AND Output | 0 | Corresponding acquired and reference waveform samples are used for AMPM measurement when both samples are greater or equal to the threshold level. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Reference Power Type | 1 | Corresponding acquired and reference waveform samples are used for AMPM measurement when reference waveform sample is greater than or equal to the threshold level and AMPM Ref Pwr Type property is set to Input. Corresponding acquired and reference waveform samples are used for AMPM measurement when acquired waveform sample is greater than or equal to the threshold level and AMPM Ref Pwr Type property is set to Output. |

## TOPIC 00126: DPD:Measurement Interval (s)

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10f004.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10f004.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the duration of the reference waveform considered for the DPD measurement. When the reference waveform contains an idle duration, the DPD measurement neglects the idle samples in the reference waveform leading up to the start of the first active portion of the reference waveform. This valu

### DPD:Measurement Interval (s)

Specifies the duration of the reference waveform considered for the DPD measurement. When the reference waveform contains an idle duration, the DPD measurement neglects the idle samples in the reference waveform leading up to the start of the first active portion of the reference waveform. This value is expressed in seconds.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is 100E-6.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | DPD Meas Interval (s) |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

## TOPIC 00130: DPD:Measurement Mode

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10f06b.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxspecan-rc/rfmxspecan/attr10f06b.html

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies if the training waveform required for the extraction of the DPD model coefficients is acquired from the hardware or is configured by the user. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic fo

### DPD:Measurement Mode

Specifies if the training waveform required for the extraction of the DPD model coefficients is acquired from the hardware or is configured by the user.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Acquire and Extract**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | DPD Meas Mode |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| Acquire and Extract | 0 | The measurement acquires the training waveform required for the extraction of the DPD model coefficients from the hardware and then computes the model coefficients. In this mode, the supported DPD Models are Lookup Table, Memory Polynomial , and Generalized Memory Polynomial. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Extract Only | 1 | The measurement uses the user configured training waveform required for the extraction of the DPD model coefficients. In this mode, the only supported DPD Model is Decomposed Vector Rotation. |

Parent topic:

RFmxSpecAn Properties

- source_description: Specifies the mode for performing the IQ measurement. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax for named signals. The default value is Normal. Remarks The f

### IQ:Measurement Mode

Specifies the mode for performing the IQ measurement.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **Normal**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | IQ Meas Mode |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| Normal | 0 | Performs the measurement in the normal RFmx execution mode and supports all the RFmx features such as overlapped measurements. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| RawIQ | 1 | Reduces the overhead introduced by this measurement by not copying and storing the data in RFmx. In this mode IQ data needs to be retrieved using RFmxInstr Fetch Raw IQ VI instead of RFmxSpecAn IQ Fetch Data VI. RFmxInstr Fetch Raw IQ directly fetches the data from the hardware. The following list describes the limitations of using this mode, No other measurements can be enabled along with this IQ measurement. You must fetch the IQ data before initiating another RFmx measurement because the data is not stored in RFmx. |

Parent topic:

### PowerList:Segment:RBW Filter:Type

| Gaussian (1) | The RBW filter has a Gaussian response. |

| None (5) | The measurement does not use any RBW filtering. |
| RRC (6) | The RRC filter with the roll-off specified by the PowerList RBW RRC Alpha property is used as the RBW filter. |

### PowerList:Segment:Trigger Type

Specifies an array of trigger type, each corresponding to a segment.

RFmx returns an error if the size of the configured values is smaller than the [Number of Segments](attr150002.html).

| None (0) | No Reference Trigger is configured. |
| --- | --- |
| Digital Edge (1) | The Reference Trigger is not asserted until a digital edge is detected. The source of the digital edge is specified using the Digital Edge Source property. |
| IQ Power Edge (2) | The Reference Trigger is asserted when the signal changes past the level specified by the slope (rising or falling), which is configured using the the IQ Power Edge Slope property. |

## TOPIC 00149: RFmxSpecAn Abort Measurements VI

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-abort-measurements-vi.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-abort-measurements-vi.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Stops acquisition and measurements associated with signal instance that you specify in the Selector String parameter, which were previously initiated by the RFmxSpecAn Initiate VI or measurement read VIs. Calling this VI is optional, unless you want to stop a measurement before it is complete. This

### RFmxSpecAn Abort Measurements VI

Stops acquisition and measurements associated with signal instance that you specify in the **Selector String** parameter, which were previously initiated by the [RFmxSpecAn Initiate](/csh?topicname=rfmxspecan-initiate-vi.html) VI or measurement read VIs. Calling this VI is optional, unless you want to stop a measurement before it is complete. This VI executes even if there is an incoming error.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmxspecan-abort-measurements-vi.png']

#### Inputs/Outputs

| Selector String — Selector String specifies a selector string comprising of the signal name. If you do not specify the signal name, the default signal instance is used. The default value is "" (empty string). Example: "" "signal::sig1" You can use the RFmxSpecAn Build Signal String VI to build the selector string. Instrument Handle In — Instrument Handle In specifies the RFmx session refnum. Instrument Handle In is obtained from the RFmxInstr Initialize NIRFSA VI. error in (no error) — error in describes error conditions that occur before this node runs. This input provides standard error in functionality. Instrument Handle Out — Instrument Handle Out passes a reference of your RFmx session to the next VI. error out — error out contains error information. This output provides standard error out functionality. |
| --- |

Parent topic:

Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-acp-configure-averaging-vi.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00150: RFmxSpecAn ACP Configure Averaging VI

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-acp-configure-averaging-vi.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-acp-configure-averaging-vi.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Configures averaging for the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement. icon Inputs/Outputs cstr.png Selector String Selector String specifies a selector string comprising of the signal name. If you do not specify the signal name, the default signal instance is used. The default value is "" (empty st

### RFmxSpecAn ACP Configure Averaging VI

Configures averaging for the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmxspecan-acp-configure-averaging-vi.png']

#### Inputs/Outputs

| Selector String — Selector String specifies a selector string comprising of the signal name. If you do not specify the signal name, the default signal instance is used. The default value is "" (empty string). Example: "" "signal::sig1" You can use the RFmxSpecAn Build Signal String VI to build the selector string. Instrument Handle In — Instrument Handle In specifies the RFmx session refnum. Instrument Handle In is obtained from the RFmxInstr Initialize NIRFSA VI. Averaging Enabled — Averaging Enabled specifies whether to enable averaging of the spectrum for the measurement. The default value is False. False (0) The measurement is performed on a single acquisition. True (1) The measurement uses the Averaging Count parameter to calculate the number of acquisitions over which the spectrum is averaged. Averaging Count — Averaging Count specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the Averaging Enabled parameter to True. The default value is 10. Averaging Type — Averaging Type specifies the averaging type for averaging multiple spectrum acquisitions. The averaged spectrum is used for the measurement. Refer to the Averaging section of the Spectral Measurements topic for more information about averaging types. The default value is RMS. RMS (0) The power spectrum is linearly averaged. RMS averaging reduces signal fluctuations but not the noise floor. Log (1) The power spectrum is averaged in a logarithmic scale. Scalar (2) The square root of the power spectrum is averaged. Max (3) The peak power in the spectrum at each frequency bin is retained from one acquisition to the next. Min (4) The least power in the spectrum at each frequency bin is retained from one acquisition to the next. error in (no error) — error in describes error conditions that occur before this node runs. This input provides standard error in functionality. Instrument Handle Out — Instrument Handle Out passes a reference of your RFmx session to the next VI. error out — error out contains error information. This output provides standard error out functionality. |  |
| --- | --- |
| False (0) | The measurement is performed on a single acquisition. |
| True (1) | The measurement uses the Averaging Count parameter to calculate the number of acquisitions over which the spectrum is averaged. |
| RMS (0) | The power spectrum is linearly averaged. RMS averaging reduces signal fluctuations but not the noise floor. |
| Log (1) | The power spectrum is averaged in a logarithmic scale. |
| Scalar (2) | The square root of the power spectrum is averaged. |
| Max (3) | The peak power in the spectrum at each frequency bin is retained from one acquisition to the next. |
| Min (4) | The least power in the spectrum at each frequency bin is retained from one acquisition to the next. |

Parent topic:

ACP

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref path=vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-acp-configure-carrier-and-offsets-vi.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00151: RFmxSpecAn ACP Configure Carrier and Offsets VI

- bundle_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-acp-configure-carrier-and-offsets-vi.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/vi-lib/rfmx/specan/mx/rfmxspecan-llb/rfmxspecan-acp-configure-carrier-and-offsets-vi.html
- document_id: `rfmxspecan-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Configures a carrier channel with offset channels on both sides of the carrier as specified by the number of offsets. The offset channels are separated by +/- n * channel spacing from the center of the carrier. Power is measured over the integration bandwidth for each channel. icon Inputs/Outputs cs

### RFmxSpecAn ACP Configure Carrier and Offsets VI

Configures a carrier channel with offset channels on both sides of the carrier as specified by the number of offsets. The offset channels are separated by +/- n * channel spacing from the center of the carrier. Power is measured over the integration bandwidth for each channel.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmxspecan-acp-configure-carrier-and-offsets-vi.png']

#### Inputs/Outputs

| Selector String — Selector String specifies a selector string comprising of the signal name. If you do not specify the signal name, the default signal instance is used. The default value is "" (empty string). Example: "" "signal::sig1" You can use the RFmxSpecAn Build Signal String VI to build the selector string. Instrument Handle In — Instrument Handle In specifies the RFmx session refnum. Instrument Handle In is obtained from the RFmxInstr Initialize NIRFSA VI. Integration Bandwidth (Hz) — Integration Bandwidth specifies the frequency range, in Hz, over which the measurement integrates the carrier channel power. The default value is 1 MHz. Number of Offsets — Number of Offsets specifies the number of offset channels. The default value is 1. Channel Spacing (Hz) — Channel Spacing specifies the spacing between offset channels. The default value is 1 MHz. error in (no error) — error in describes error conditions that occur before this node runs. This input provides standard error in functionality. Instrument Handle Out — Instrument Handle Out passes a reference of your RFmx session to the next VI. error out — error out contains error information. This output provides standard error out functionality. |
| --- |

### RFmxSpecAn ACP Configure Carrier Mode VI

Configures whether to consider the carrier power as part of total carrier power measurement.

Use "carrier<*n*>" as the selector string to configure this VI.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmxspecan-acp-configure-carrier-mode-vi.png']

#### Inputs/Outputs

| Selector String — Selector String specifies a selector string comprising of the signal name and carrier number. If you do not specify the signal name, the default signal instance is used. The default value is "carrier0". Example: "carrier0" "signal::sig1/carrier0" You can use the RFmxSpecAn Build Carrier String2 VI to build the selector string. Instrument Handle In — Instrument Handle In specifies the RFmx session refnum. Instrument Handle In is obtained from the RFmxInstr Initialize NIRFSA VI. Carrier Mode — Carrier Mode specifies whether to consider the carrier power as part of total carrier power measurement. The default value is Active. Passive (0) The carrier power is not considered as part of total carrier power. Active (1) The carrier power is considered as part of total carrier power. error in (no error) — error in describes error conditions that occur before this node runs. This input provides standard error in functionality. Instrument Handle Out — Instrument Handle Out passes a reference of your RFmx session to the next VI. error out — error out contains error information. This output provides standard error out functionality. |  |
| --- | --- |
| Passive (0) | The carrier power is not considered as part of total carrier power. |
| Active (1) | The carrier power is considered as part of total carrier power. |

The noise floor of the signal analyzer is measured for the RF path used by the ACP measurement and cached for future use. If signal analyzer or measurement parameters change, noise floors are measured again. The noise floor of the signal analyzer is measured for the RF path used by the ACP measurement and cached for future use. If signal analyzer or measurement parameters change, noise floors are measured again. Supported Devices: PXIe-5663/5665/5668, PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5842/5860 |
